<div id="review_909991955" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/909991955" />
    <a title="Terri Wino" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28305082-terri-wino"><img alt="Terri Wino" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483376205p2/28305082.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/909991955?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Terri Wino" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Terri Wino" href="/user/show/28305082-terri-wino">Terri Wino</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28305082-terri-wino?shelf=year-2014">year-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer909991955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer202011187791079307">Catherine McKenzie gives good "Chick Lit!!" This is the second book I've read by her -- Forgotten being the first -- and I thoroughly enjoyed both!<br/>In part 1 of the book we meet Anne, a woman frustrated with failed relationships who, on a whim, decides to visit a dating service. However, she is shocked to discover that it is actually an arranged marriage service. Of course, she decides to go through with it...that's the point of the book after all.<br/>Part 2 of the book is Anne meeting and getting to</span>
  <span id="freeText202011187791079307" style="display:none">Catherine McKenzie gives good "Chick Lit!!" This is the second book I've read by her -- Forgotten being the first -- and I thoroughly enjoyed both!<br />In part 1 of the book we meet Anne, a woman frustrated with failed relationships who, on a whim, decides to visit a dating service. However, she is shocked to discover that it is actually an arranged marriage service. Of course, she decides to go through with it...that's the point of the book after all.<br />Part 2 of the book is Anne meeting and getting to know her husband-to-be. Jack is so not the type, physically or personality-wise, that is her past pattern. I love their struggle to figure out what the heck they're thinking, to actually do this thing. Basically, marry a complete stranger that some agency is telling you you're a good match with.<br />Then comes part 3 of the book, which threw me for a loop because I honestly didn't see it coming. But it grabbed my interest and sucked me back in just when I was thinking, "Well, we know how the rest of this formula is going to play out."<br />Are there things that happen in this book that are way too convenient (like getting the money for the large fee the agency charges for their service)? Yep. Did it take away from the story for me? Nope!<br />Do you KNOW how this story is going to eventually end? Of course. BUT I loved that story that brought me to the end!<br />I really liked both Anne and Jack. I was happy when they were happy. I was angry and upset when they were.<br />Catherine McKenzie has a way of making you feel as if you're a part of her characters. She draws you into their world, and it's a fun place to be for the duration of their story. <br />I definitely will be reading her other books. If you enjoy romance that's not the typical girl-meets-guy, cookie-cutter formula, and like quirky characters, you should read her books too!</span>
  <a data-text-id="202011187791079307" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_316943051" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/316943051" />
    <a title="Kelly Hager" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1436215-kelly-hager"><img alt="Kelly Hager" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1422502668p2/1436215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/316943051?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly Hager" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly Hager" href="/user/show/1436215-kelly-hager">Kelly Hager</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781554687602" href="/book/show/8590382-arranged">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer316943051" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8224062409644423109">After her latest relationship ends, Anne Blythe* is unsure of what to do. She wants to get married and have kids, but she keeps picking the wrong guys. She finds a business card for what she thinks is a dating service. When she finally decides to give it a try, she learns it's a company that actually creates arranged marriages.<br/><br/>Even so, she eventually decides to go for it and when she meets Jack, there is an instant connection. But can there be a happy ending when you marry a stranger?<br/><br/>I don't kno</span>
  <span id="freeText8224062409644423109" style="display:none">After her latest relationship ends, Anne Blythe* is unsure of what to do. She wants to get married and have kids, but she keeps picking the wrong guys. She finds a business card for what she thinks is a dating service. When she finally decides to give it a try, she learns it's a company that actually creates arranged marriages.<br /><br />Even so, she eventually decides to go for it and when she meets Jack, there is an instant connection. But can there be a happy ending when you marry a stranger?<br /><br />I don't know that I would have picked this book for review if I hadn't already read and loved her earlier book, Spin. I don't read the literary equivalent of romantic comedies very often. But I DID love Spin and I was pretty sure that Catherine McKenzie would pull this off, too. (Spoiler: she did.)<br /><br />Yes, this book is fluffy and sounds like a really bad Katherine Heigl movie. But it's incredibly funny and smart and Anne is a wonderful narrator.<br /><br />And Anne is fantastic. Yes, she rushes into things without considering potential consequences, but she's also a wonderful person---good at her job, fiercely loyal to her friends and someone who loves completely. So while she's got flaws, she's also more than the sum total of those flaws.<br /><br />The love story between Jack and Anne is rushed (and unconventional, to say the least) but it also feels genuine. And that is what I love about Catherine McKenzie's books. The synopses sound like other books (or movies) but when I read them, they are so realistic and, yes, genuine.<br /><br />Highly recommended. I cannot wait for her next book.<br /><br />* = not a coincidence. Her full name is Anne Shirley Blythe.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8224062409644423109" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_302836936" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/302836936" />
    <a title="Laurel-Rain" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1402123-laurel-rain"><img alt="Laurel-Rain" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591104726p2/1402123.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/302836936?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurel-Rain" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurel-Rain" href="/user/show/1402123-laurel-rain">Laurel-Rain</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer302836936" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15808494812744637069">Anne Blythe is the kind of woman who believes in love. She wants the whole fairytale thing, even though, so far, none of her relationships have worked out. Something always goes wrong.<br/><br/>Meanwhile, she does have so many other good things in her life: a great job as a writer at a magazine; a potential book deal; and really good friends.<br/><br/>So why can't she have it all? When her best friend Sarah announces her engagement, Anne does something completely out of character. She calls an agency that she belie</span>
  <span id="freeText15808494812744637069" style="display:none">Anne Blythe is the kind of woman who believes in love. She wants the whole fairytale thing, even though, so far, none of her relationships have worked out. Something always goes wrong.<br /><br />Meanwhile, she does have so many other good things in her life: a great job as a writer at a magazine; a potential book deal; and really good friends.<br /><br />So why can't she have it all? When her best friend Sarah announces her engagement, Anne does something completely out of character. She calls an agency that she believes to be a dating service and makes an appointment. But imagine her surprise when she discovers that the agency arranges marriages.<br /><br />Who in this modern age would fall for something like that? But since nothing else has worked, why not?<br /><br />Fast forward a few months. After doing some research, taking psychological tests, and undergoing the requisite counseling, Anne finds herself at a Mexican resort meeting her match, Jack H. Surprisingly, even though he isn't her usual type, she finds herself drawn to him. He, too, is a writer and has gone through several unsuccessful relationships. And isn't she trying to change her type? Isn't this bold experiment all about finding a compatible friend?<br /><br />The two are married and return to Manhattan to begin their lives: moving in together, finding their rhythm, and falling in love. Or so Anne believes.<br /><br />But then something blindsides Anne when she discovers Jack's secret work-in-progress.<br /><br />What mysteries lie within the pages of Jack's manuscript that turn her world upside down? What does she do next? And how will she go on after this bitter betrayal?<br /><br />From this point until the end, this unique tale turns a bit predictable. However, "Arranged: A Novel" was one of those books that I had to keep reading, just because I wasn't completely sure how it would end. And because I had really connected with the characters. Anne is the kind of woman often portrayed in books and movies: successful, attractive, and hoping to find love. The kind of character that could be a friend or family member. Jack is also the kind of character that attracts female readers with his mix of sensitivity and masculinity. And because her characters are so real, McKenzie kept my interest until the final page. Four stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15808494812744637069" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ma5dcEfE0JsGm/Nvh4n6JUQxucu3w/5ItUmDGFzxAdyJ3MGSc64g6pyhExzy54K4BHAYvrzxXFA6YFO8P8VgjA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('a8GENAe5iopBxcUjbquV/DgZOgPxUWILACTgB7r9Okp7sxjWM9N6+9v/JVAbxe1heFibdvpjwBOPDTCj2clbGg==')})
  }

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9113775142850462417">Catherine McKenzie was born and raised in Montreal, Canada. A graduate of McGill in History and Law, Catherine practiced law in Montreal for twenty years before retiring to write full time. An avid runner and skier, she's the author of numerous bestsellers including HIDDEN, FRACTURED, THE GOOD LIAR and I'LL NEVER TELL. Her works have been translated into multiple languages.<br/><br/>In 2019, I'LL NEVER TELL</span>
  <span id="freeText9113775142850462417" style="display:none">Catherine McKenzie was born and raised in Montreal, Canada. A graduate of McGill in History and Law, Catherine practiced law in Montreal for twenty years before retiring to write full time. An avid runner and skier, she's the author of numerous bestsellers including HIDDEN, FRACTURED, THE GOOD LIAR and I'LL NEVER TELL. Her works have been translated into multiple languages.<br /><br />In 2019, I'LL NEVER TELL was a #1 Amazon Bestseller, a Globe &amp; Mail and Toronto Star Bestseller, was shortlisted for the Hugh McLennan Prize for Fiction and was optioned for a television series by Paramount TV. Her latest novel, YOU CAN'T CATCH ME released June 9, 2020 and has also been optioned by Paramount TV.<br /><br />Her next novel, SIX WEEKS TO LIVE, will be released on May 4, 2021.</span>
